}
}
});
}
worker = new Worker(URL.createObjectURL(new Blob(["var interval; self.addEventListener('message', function(msg){ switch(msg.data){ case 'start': interval = setInterval(function(){ self.postMessage('tick'); }, 50); break; case 'stop': clearInterval(interval); break; }});"], {type:'text/javascript'})));
worker.addEventListener("message", Main);
video.addEventListener("play", function(){
worker.postMessage("start");
});
output_canvas.addEventListener("click", function(e){
let rect = output_canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
let x = e.clientX - rect.left;
let y = e.clientY - rect.top;
if(x < 90 && y < 40) difficulty = Math.floor(x / 45);
else if(synth_utter != undefined && 100 < x && x < 145 && 200 < y && y < 245) synth_utter.volume = synth_utter.volume ? 0 : 1;
});
pip_button.addEventListener("click", function() {
if (document.pictureInPictureElement) document.exitPictureInPicture();
else pip_video.requestPictureInPicture();
});
capture_button.addEventListener("click", ScreenCapture);
}
else{
document.body.innerHTML = "";
alert("지원하지 않는 브라우저입니다.");
}
function ScreenCapture(){
if(output_canvas.style.display == "none"){
navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia({
audio: false,
video: true
}).then(function(mediaStream){
output_canvas.style.display = "block";
video.srcObject = mediaStream;
if(document.pictureInPictureEnabled){
pip_button.style.display = "block";
pip_video.srcObject = output_canvas.captureStream();
}
mediaStream.getVideoTracks()[0].addEventListener("ended", function(){
output_canvas.style.display = "none";
pip_button.style.display = "none";
worker.postMessage("stop");
if(document.pictureInPictureElement) document.exitPictureInPicture();
});
});
}
}
function Speak(text){
if(synth_utter != undefined && synth_utter.text != text){
synth.cancel();
synth_utter.text = text;
synth.speak(synth_utter);
}
}
function Time(data){
let segment_value = new Array(4);
let segment_start = [0,20,67,88];
let segment_pos = [[7,13], [0,7], [0,19], [7,26], [13,19], [13,7], [7,0]]; //g, f, e ,d, c, b, a
for(let i = 0; i < segment_start.length; i++){
for(let j = 0; j <= 8; j++){
for(let k = 0; k <= 8; k++){
let f1 = (segment_start[i] + 4 + j + 105 * (k + 4)) * 4;
let f2 = (segment_start[i] + 4 + j + 105 * (k + 17)) * 4;
if((data[f1] + data[f1 + 1] + data[f1 + 2]) / 3 > 127 || (data[f2] + data[f2 + 1] + data[f2 + 2]) / 3 > 127) return undefined;
}
}
let segment_display = 0;
for(let j = 0; j < segment_pos.length; j++){
let f1 = (segment_start[i] + segment_pos[j][0] + 105 * segment_pos[j][1]) * 4;
let col = (data[f1] + data[f1 + 1] + data[f1 + 2]) / 3 > 127;
for(let k = segment_pos[j][0]; k < segment_pos[j][0] + 4; k++){
for(let l = segment_pos[j][1]; l < segment_pos[j][1] + 4; l++){
let f2 = (segment_start[i] + k + 105 * l) * 4;
if(col != (data[f2] + data[f2 + 1] + data[f2 + 2]) / 3 > 127) return undefined;
}
}
if(col) segment_display += 1 << j;
}
switch(segment_display){
case 126: segment_value[i] = 0; break;
case 48: segment_value[i] = 1; break;
case 109: segment_value[i] = 2; break;
case 121: segment_value[i] = 3; break;
case 51: segment_value[i] = 4; break;
case 91: segment_value[i] = 5; break;
case 95: segment_value[i] = 6; break;
case 112: segment_value[i] = 7; break;
case 127: segment_value[i] = 8; break;
case 123: segment_value[i] = 9; break;
default:
if(i == 0 && segment_display == 0) segment_value[i] = 0;
else return undefined;
}
}
return (segment_value[0] * 10 + segment_value[1]) * 60 + segment_value[2] * 10 + segment_value[3];
}
function Visit(area, x, y, data, visited){
let len = data.length / 4;
let pos = x + y * 22;
if(pos < 0 || pos >= len || visited[pos]) return;
visited[pos] = true;
if((data[pos * 4] + data[pos * 4 + 1] + data[pos * 4 + 2]) / 3 > 127){
area[0] = Math.min(x, area[0]);
area[1] = Math.max(x, area[1]);
area[2] = Math.min(y, area[2]);
area[3] = Math.max(y, area[3]);
for(let i = -1; i <= 1; i++){
for(let j = -1; j <= 1; j++){
Visit(area, x + i, y + j, data, visited);
}
}
}
}
function Hp(data){
let len = data.length / 4;
let visited = new Array(len).fill(false);
let hex_char = "0123456789abcdef";
let rslt = "";
for(let i = len - 1; i >= 0; i--){
if(!visited[i]){
if((data[i * 4] + data[i * 4 + 1] + data[i * 4 + 2]) / 3 > 127){
let origin_y = Math.floor(i / 22);
let origin_x = i - origin_y * 22;
let area = [origin_x, origin_x, origin_y, origin_y];
Visit(area, origin_x, origin_y, data, visited);
if(area[1] - area[0] + 1 > 5 || area[3] - area[2] + 1 > 7) return undefined;
let hex = new Array(12).fill(0);
for(let j = area[0]; j <= area[1]; j++){
for(let k = area[2]; k <= area[3]; k++){
let pos = j + k * 22;
if((data[pos * 4] + data[pos * 4 + 1] + data[pos * 4 + 2]) / 3 > 127){
let x = j - area[0];
let y = k - area[2];
hex[Math.floor(x / 2) + Math.floor(y / 2) * 3] += 1 << (x % 2 + (y % 2) * 2);
}
}
}
let hex_str = "";
for(let j = 0; j < hex.length; j++) hex_str += hex_char[hex[j]];
switch(hex_str){
case "100000000000":
if(rslt.length != 1) return undefined;
rslt = "." + rslt; break;
case "634505505230": rslt = "0" + rslt; break;
case "e00a00a00200": rslt = "1" + rslt; break;
case "634081810331": rslt = "2" + rslt; break;
case "6340c1405230": rslt = "3" + rslt; break;
case "0e06a03b1020": rslt = "4" + rslt; break;
case "7319c0405230": rslt = "5" + rslt; break;
case "634dc0505230": rslt = "6" + rslt; break;
case "335081060010": rslt = "7" + rslt; break;
case "6349c1505230": rslt = "8" + rslt; break;
case "6349c5405230": rslt = "9" + rslt; break;
default: return undefined;
}
}
else visited[i] = true;
}
}
if(rslt != "100" && rslt.indexOf(".") <= 0) return undefined;
return parseFloat(rslt);
}
function Detect(data){
let cnt = 0;
for(let i = 0; i < data.length / 4; i++){
let r = Math.max(0, Math.floor(data[i * 4] * (3 / 256)) * 128 - 1);
let g = Math.max(0, Math.floor(data[i * 4 + 1] * (3 / 256)) * 128 - 1);
let b = Math.max(0, Math.floor(data[i * 4 + 2] * (3 / 256)) * 128 - 1);
if(r > 127 && g + b == 0) cnt++;
}
if(cnt > 4000) return true;
return false;
}
function Main(){
let canvas_width = canvas.width;
canvas.width = video.videoWidth;
let resize = Math.abs(canvas.width - canvas_width) > 50;
canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
output_ctx.textBaseline = "top";
output_ctx.drawImage(output_canvas_bg, 0, 0, output_canvas.width, output_canvas.height);
output_ctx.font = "15pt Nanum Gothic";
output_ctx.textAlign = "left";
output_ctx.fillStyle = difficulty ? "#FFFFFF40" : "#FFFFFF";
output_ctx.fillText("노말", 5, 12);
output_ctx.fillStyle = difficulty ? "#FFFFFF" : "#FFFFFF40";
output_ctx.fillText("하드", 50, 12);
if(synth_utter != undefined) output_ctx.drawImage(synth_utter.volume ? unmute_img : mute_img, 108, 208, 32,32);
if(resize) caption_height = undefined;
if(caption_height == undefined){
for(let i = 0; i <= 50; i++){
let time_frame = ctx.getImageData(canvas.width / 2 - 23, i + 42, 105, 30);
if(Time(time_frame.data) != undefined){
caption_height = i;
break;
}
}
}else{
let time_frame = ctx.getImageData(canvas.width / 2 - 23, caption_height + 42, 105, 30);
let hp_frame = ctx.getImageData(canvas.width / 2 - 397, caption_height + 40, 22, 12);
let detect_frame = ctx.getImageData(canvas.width / 2 - 362, caption_height + 19, 760, 12);
let time_rslt = Time(time_frame.data);
if(time_rslt != undefined && time_rslt != time){
time_stamp = Date.now();
time = time_rslt;
}
let hp_rslt = Hp(hp_frame.data);
if(hp_rslt != undefined) hp = hp_rslt;
if(time != undefined){
let millis = (Date.now() - time_stamp) / 1000;
let curr_time = time - Math.floor(millis);
if(Detect(detect_frame.data)){
latest_pattern_time = curr_time + (Math.floor(millis) == Math.round(millis) ? 2 : 1);
uncertain = hp == 61 || hp == 31;
if(hp < 31) pattern_cycle = 2;
else if(hp < 61) pattern_cycle = 1;
else pattern_cycle = 0;
}
output_ctx.textAlign = "center";
let estimated_time = [latest_pattern_time - pattern_cycles[difficulty][pattern_cycle]];
if(uncertain){
let uncertain_estimated_time = estimated_time[0] + (pattern_cycles[difficulty][0] - pattern_cycles[difficulty][1])
if(curr_time - uncertain_estimated_time >= 0) estimated_time.push(uncertain_estimated_time);
}
for(let i = 0; i < estimated_time.length; i++){
if(estimated_time[i] < 0) continue;
let remaining_time = Math.max(0, curr_time - estimated_time[i]);
if(i == 0 && remaining_time > 0){
if(remaining_time <= 10) Speak(remaining_time);
else if((remaining_time < 60 && remaining_time % 10 == 0) || remaining_time % 30 == 0){
let minutes = Math.floor(remaining_time / 60);
let seconds = remaining_time - minutes * 60;
Speak((minutes > 0 ? minutes + "분 " : "") + (seconds > 0 ? seconds + "초 " : "") + "남았습니다." + (estimated_time.length > 1 ? " 패턴이 더 빨리 올 가능성이 있습니다." : ""));
}
}
output_ctx.font = (estimated_time.length > 1 ? 20 : 30) + "pt Nanum Gothic";
output_ctx.fillStyle = remaining_time > 10 ? "#000000" : "#FF0000";
output_ctx.strokeStyle = "#FFFFFF";
output_ctx.lineWidth = 1;
let txt = remaining_time + "초 후";
output_ctx.fillText(txt, 125, 145 + (estimated_time.length > 1 ? (i == 0 ? 25 : -55) : 0));
output_ctx.strokeText(txt, 125, 145 + (estimated_time.length > 1 ? (i == 0 ? 25 : -55) : 0));
output_ctx.font = (estimated_time.length > 1 ? 30 : 35) + "pt Nanum Gothic";
output_ctx.fillStyle = "#FFFFFF";
output_ctx.strokeStyle = "#000000";
output_ctx.lineWidth = 2;
let minutes = Math.floor(estimated_time[i] / 60);
let seconds = estimated_time[i] - minutes * 60;
txt = (minutes < 10 ? "0" : "") + minutes + "분 " + (seconds < 10 ? "0" : "") + seconds + "초";
output_ctx.fillText(txt, 125, 90 + (estimated_time.length > 1 ? (i == 0 ? 35 : -45) : 0));
output_ctx.strokeText(txt, 125, 90 + (estimated_time.length > 1 ? (i == 0 ? 35 : -45) : 0));
}
output_ctx.font = "10pt Nanum Gothic";
output_ctx.textAlign = "left";
output_ctx.fillStyle = "#FFFFFF";
if(time_rslt == undefined) output_ctx.fillStyle += "40";
output_ctx.fillText("남은 시간", 5, 215);
curr_time = Math.max(0, curr_time);
let minutes = Math.floor(curr_time / 60);
let seconds = curr_time - minutes * 60;
output_ctx.fillText((minutes < 10 ? "0" : "") + minutes + "분 " + (seconds < 10 ? "0" : "") + seconds + "초", 5, 230);
output_ctx.textAlign = "right";
output_ctx.fillStyle = "#FFFFFF";
if(hp_rslt == undefined) output_ctx.fillStyle += "40";
output_ctx.fillText("남은 체력", 245, 215);
output_ctx.fillText(hp + "%", 245, 230);
}
}
}
</script>
</body>
